;-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
; => Constants
;-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
f        = !VALUES.F_NAN
d        = !VALUES.D_NAN
c        = 2.99792458d8      ; -Speed of light in vacuum (m/s)
kB       = 1.380658d-23      ; -Boltzmann Constant (J/K)
epo      = 8.854187817d-12   ; -Permittivity of free space (F/m)
muo      = 4d0*!DPI*1d-7     ; -Permeability of free space (N/A^2 or H/m)
me       = 9.1093897d-31     ; -Electron mass (kg)
mp       = 1.6726231d-27     ; -Proton mass (kg)
qq       = 1.60217733d-19    ; => Fundamental charge (C)

date     = '121097'
test0    = tdss_lhw_stats_read(DATE=date)
avg_lfk0 = (test0.K_ST_LOWF_MP + test0.K_EN_LOWF_MP)/2d0
avg_hfk0 = (test0.K_ST_highF_MP + test0.K_EN_highF_MP)/2d0
freql0   = test0.FREQ_LOW_HIGH[*,0]
freqh0   = test0.FREQ_LOW_HIGH[*,1]
thkb0    = test0.THETA_KB
thkv0    = test0.THETA_KV
pkamp0   = test0.PEAK_AMP
thkbav0  = (test0.THETA_KB[*,0] + test0.THETA_KB[*,1])/2d0   ; => Avg. between start and end
thkvav0  = (test0.THETA_KV[*,0] + test0.THETA_KV[*,1])/2d0   ; => Avg. between start and end
wce0     = (test0.WCE_SE[*,0] + test0.WCE_SE[*,1])/2d0
wpe0     = (test0.WPE_SE[*,0] + test0.WPE_SE[*,1])/2d0
wlh0     = (test0.WLH_SE[*,0] + test0.WLH_SE[*,1])/2d0
vte0     = (test0.VTE_SE[*,0] + test0.VTE_SE[*,1])/2d0
rhoe0    = (test0.RHO_VTCE_SE[*,0] + test0.RHO_VTCE_SE[*,1])/2d0
thkb0    = (thkb0) < (18d1 - thkb0)
thkv0    = (thkv0) < (18d1 - thkv0)
thkb0    = (thkb0[*,0] + thkb0[*,1])/2d0
thkv0    = (thkv0[*,0] + thkv0[*,1])/2d0
vsw0     = (test0.VSW_ST + test0.VSW_EN)/2d0
magf0    = (test0.MAGF_ST + test0.MAGF_EN)/2d0
dens0    = (test0.NE_SE[*,0] + test0.NE_SE[*,1])/2d0
bmag0    = SQRT(TOTAL(magf0^2,2L,/NAN))

date     = '082698'
test1    = tdss_lhw_stats_read(DATE=date)
avg_lfk1 = (test1.K_ST_LOWF_MP + test1.K_EN_LOWF_MP)/2d0
avg_hfk1 = (test1.K_ST_highF_MP + test1.K_EN_highF_MP)/2d0
freql1   = test1.FREQ_LOW_HIGH[*,0]
freqh1   = test1.FREQ_LOW_HIGH[*,1]
thkb1    = test1.THETA_KB
thkv1    = test1.THETA_KV
pkamp1   = test1.PEAK_AMP
thkbav1  = (test1.THETA_KB[*,0] + test1.THETA_KB[*,1])/2d0   ; => Avg. between start and end
thkvav1  = (test1.THETA_KV[*,0] + test1.THETA_KV[*,1])/2d0   ; => Avg. between start and end
wce1     = (test1.WCE_SE[*,0] + test1.WCE_SE[*,1])/2d0
wpe1     = (test1.WPE_SE[*,0] + test1.WPE_SE[*,1])/2d0
wlh1     = (test1.WLH_SE[*,0] + test1.WLH_SE[*,1])/2d0
vte1     = (test1.VTE_SE[*,0] + test1.VTE_SE[*,1])/2d0
rhoe1    = (test1.RHO_VTCE_SE[*,0] + test1.RHO_VTCE_SE[*,1])/2d0
thkb1    = (thkb1) < (18d1 - thkb1)
thkv1    = (thkv1) < (18d1 - thkv1)
thkb1    = (thkb1[*,0] + thkb1[*,1])/2d0
thkv1    = (thkv1[*,0] + thkv1[*,1])/2d0
vsw1     = (test1.VSW_ST + test1.VSW_EN)/2d0
magf1    = (test1.MAGF_ST + test1.MAGF_EN)/2d0
dens1    = (test1.NE_SE[*,0] + test1.NE_SE[*,1])/2d0
bmag1    = SQRT(TOTAL(magf1^2,2L,/NAN))

date     = '092498'
test2    = tdss_lhw_stats_read(DATE=date)
avg_lfk2 = (test2.K_ST_LOWF_MP + test2.K_EN_LOWF_MP)/2d0
avg_hfk2 = (test2.K_ST_highF_MP + test2.K_EN_highF_MP)/2d0
freql2   = test2.FREQ_LOW_HIGH[*,0]
freqh2   = test2.FREQ_LOW_HIGH[*,1]
thkb2    = test2.THETA_KB
thkv2    = test2.THETA_KV
pkamp2   = test2.PEAK_AMP
thkbav2  = (test2.THETA_KB[*,0] + test2.THETA_KB[*,1])/2d0   ; => Avg. between start and end
thkvav2  = (test2.THETA_KV[*,0] + test2.THETA_KV[*,1])/2d0   ; => Avg. between start and end
wce2     = (test2.WCE_SE[*,0] + test2.WCE_SE[*,1])/2d0
wpe2     = (test2.WPE_SE[*,0] + test2.WPE_SE[*,1])/2d0
wlh2     = (test2.WLH_SE[*,0] + test2.WLH_SE[*,1])/2d0
vte2     = (test2.VTE_SE[*,0] + test2.VTE_SE[*,1])/2d0
rhoe2    = (test2.RHO_VTCE_SE[*,0] + test2.RHO_VTCE_SE[*,1])/2d0
thkb2    = (thkb2) < (18d1 - thkb2)
thkv2    = (thkv2) < (18d1 - thkv2)
thkb2    = (thkb2[*,0] + thkb2[*,1])/2d0
thkv2    = (thkv2[*,0] + thkv2[*,1])/2d0
vsw2     = (test2.VSW_ST + test2.VSW_EN)/2d0
magf2    = (test2.MAGF_ST + test2.MAGF_EN)/2d0
dens2    = (test2.NE_SE[*,0] + test2.NE_SE[*,1])/2d0
bmag2    = SQRT(TOTAL(magf2^2,2L,/NAN))

date     = '021100'
test3    = tdss_lhw_stats_read(DATE=date)
avg_lfk3 = (test3.K_ST_LOWF_MP + test3.K_EN_LOWF_MP)/2d0
avg_hfk3 = (test3.K_ST_highF_MP + test3.K_EN_highF_MP)/2d0
freql3   = test3.FREQ_LOW_HIGH[*,0]
freqh3   = test3.FREQ_LOW_HIGH[*,1]
thkb3    = test3.THETA_KB
thkv3    = test3.THETA_KV
pkamp3   = test3.PEAK_AMP
thkbav3  = (test3.THETA_KB[*,0] + test3.THETA_KB[*,1])/2d0   ; => Avg. between start and end
thkvav3  = (test3.THETA_KV[*,0] + test3.THETA_KV[*,1])/2d0   ; => Avg. between start and end
wce3     = (test3.WCE_SE[*,0] + test3.WCE_SE[*,1])/2d0
wpe3     = (test3.WPE_SE[*,0] + test3.WPE_SE[*,1])/2d0
wlh3     = (test3.WLH_SE[*,0] + test3.WLH_SE[*,1])/2d0
vte3     = (test3.VTE_SE[*,0] + test3.VTE_SE[*,1])/2d0
rhoe3    = (test3.RHO_VTCE_SE[*,0] + test3.RHO_VTCE_SE[*,1])/2d0
thkb3    = (thkb3) < (18d1 - thkb3)
thkv3    = (thkv3) < (18d1 - thkv3)
thkb3    = (thkb3[*,0] + thkb3[*,1])/2d0
thkv3    = (thkv3[*,0] + thkv3[*,1])/2d0
vsw3     = (test3.VSW_ST + test3.VSW_EN)/2d0
magf3    = (test3.MAGF_ST + test3.MAGF_EN)/2d0
dens3    = (test3.NE_SE[*,0] + test3.NE_SE[*,1])/2d0
bmag3    = SQRT(TOTAL(magf3^2,2L,/NAN))
;-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
; => Combine terms
;-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
thkb     = [thkb0,thkb1,thkb2,thkb3]
thkv     = [thkv0,thkv1,thkv2,thkv3]
vsw      = [vsw0,vsw1,vsw2,vsw3]
vmag     = SQRT(TOTAL(vsw^2,2L,/NAN))
freql    = [freql0,freql1,freql2,freql3]
freqh    = [freqh0,freqh1,freqh2,freqh3]
wce      = [wce0,wce1,wce2,wce3]
wcp      = wce*me/mp
wx1      = SQRT(2d0)*wcp            ; => Cross-over frequency
wpe      = [wpe0,wpe1,wpe2,wpe3]
wlh      = [wlh0,wlh1,wlh2,wlh3]
vte      = [vte0,vte1,vte2,vte3]
rhoe     = [rhoe0,rhoe1,rhoe2,rhoe3]
avg_lfk  = [avg_lfk0,avg_lfk1,avg_lfk2,avg_lfk3]
avg_hfk  = [avg_hfk0,avg_hfk1,avg_hfk2,avg_hfk3]
dens     = [dens0,dens1,dens2,dens3]
bmag     = [bmag0,bmag1,bmag2,bmag3]

kcwpelfm = avg_lfk[*,0]*c*1d-3/wpe
kcwpelfp = avg_lfk[*,1]*c*1d-3/wpe
kcwpehfm = avg_hfk[*,0]*c*1d-3/wpe
kcwpehfp = avg_hfk[*,1]*c*1d-3/wpe

krhoelfm = avg_lfk[*,0]*rhoe
krhoelfp = avg_lfk[*,1]*rhoe
krhoehfm = avg_hfk[*,0]*rhoe
krhoehfp = avg_hfk[*,1]*rhoe
; => Separate by plus and minus sign
avg_lfkm = avg_lfk[*,0]
avg_lfkp = avg_lfk[*,1]
avg_hfkm = avg_hfk[*,0]
avg_hfkp = avg_hfk[*,1]
; => Calculate rest frame frequencies
ckm        = (c*1d-3)
fac0       = wce*COS(thkb*!DPI/18d1)
fac1lm     = (wpe/(ckm*avg_lfkm))^2
fac1lp     = (wpe/(ckm*avg_lfkp))^2
fac1hm     = (wpe/(ckm*avg_hfkm))^2
fac1hp     = (wpe/(ckm*avg_hfkp))^2
frest_lfkm = fac0/(1d0 + fac1lm)
frest_lfkp = fac0/(1d0 + fac1lp)
frest_hfkm = fac0/(1d0 + fac1hm)
frest_hfkp = fac0/(1d0 + fac1hp)

;frest_lfkm = avg_lfkm^2*fac0/(wpe^2 + (avg_lfkm*ckm)^2)
;frest_lfkp = avg_lfkp^2*fac0/(wpe^2 + (avg_lfkp*ckm)^2)
;frest_hfkm = avg_hfkm^2*fac0/(wpe^2 + (avg_hfkm*ckm)^2)
;frest_hfkp = avg_hfkp^2*fac0/(wpe^2 + (avg_hfkp*ckm)^2)
; => Calculate index of refraction
;indexlm  = (avg_lfkm*ckm)^2/(frest_lfkm)^2
;indexlp  = (avg_lfkp*ckm)^2/(frest_lfkp)^2
;indexhm  = (avg_hfkm*ckm)^2/(frest_hfkm)^2
;indexhp  = (avg_hfkp*ckm)^2/(frest_hfkp)^2

; => Calculate index of refraction
testlm   = cold_plasma_params_2d(bmag,dens,FREQF=frest_lfkm/(2d0*!DPI),ANGLE=thkb,/ONED)
testlp   = cold_plasma_params_2d(bmag,dens,FREQF=frest_lfkp/(2d0*!DPI),ANGLE=thkb,/ONED)
testhm   = cold_plasma_params_2d(bmag,dens,FREQF=frest_hfkm/(2d0*!DPI),ANGLE=thkb,/ONED)
testhp   = cold_plasma_params_2d(bmag,dens,FREQF=frest_hfkp/(2d0*!DPI),ANGLE=thkb,/ONED)
indexlm  = testlm.INDEX_REF_1
alfvinlm = testlm.INDEX_ALFVEN
bad      = WHERE(indexlm LT 0.,bd)
IF (bd GT 0) THEN indexlm[bad] = d
indexlp  = testlp.INDEX_REF_1
alfvinlp = testlp.INDEX_ALFVEN
bad      = WHERE(indexlp LT 0.,bd)
IF (bd GT 0) THEN indexlp[bad] = d
indexhm  = testhm.INDEX_REF_1
alfvinhm = testhm.INDEX_ALFVEN
bad      = WHERE(indexhm LT 0.,bd)
IF (bd GT 0) THEN indexhm[bad] = d
indexhp  = testhp.INDEX_REF_1
alfvinhp = testhp.INDEX_ALFVEN
bad      = WHERE(indexhp LT 0.,bd)
IF (bd GT 0) THEN indexhp[bad] = d

PRINT,";", MIN(indexlm,/NAN), MAX(indexlm,/NAN), MIN(indexlm/alfvinlm,/NAN), MAX(indexlm/alfvinlm,/NAN)
;       52508.134   2.9077398e+10    0.0059691250       10148.666
PRINT,";", MIN(indexlp,/NAN), MAX(indexlp,/NAN), MIN(indexlp/alfvinlp,/NAN), MAX(indexlp/alfvinlp,/NAN)
;       41657.192       11721740.    0.0049038669      0.95970483
PRINT,";", MIN(indexhm,/NAN), MAX(indexhm,/NAN), MIN(indexhm/alfvinhm,/NAN), MAX(indexhm/alfvinhm,/NAN)
;       16964.921       11255488.    0.0027573224       1.0004883
PRINT,";", MIN(indexhp,/NAN), MAX(indexhp,/NAN), MIN(indexhp/alfvinhp,/NAN), MAX(indexhp/alfvinhp,/NAN)
;       16113.280       12161923.    0.0025930528      0.99574439


test     = cold_plasma_params_2d(bmag,dens,FREQF=frest_lfkm/(2d0*!DPI),ANGLE=thkb,/ONED)
PRINT,";", indexlm[0], test.INDEX_REF_0[0], test.INDEX_REF_1[0]
;       9001232.9      -36020533.       9001232.9

PRINT,";", indexlm[0]/test.INDEX_ALFVEN[0], $
           test.INDEX_REF_0[0]/test.INDEX_ALFVEN[0], test.INDEX_REF_1[0]/test.INDEX_ALFVEN[0]
;      0.64861945      -2.5956020      0.64861945

PRINT,";", indexlm[0]/test.INDEX_REF_0[0], indexlm[0]/test.INDEX_REF_1[0]
;     -0.24989172       1.0000000

;-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
; => Determine a cut off
;-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
nvals    = N_ELEMENTS(WHERE(FINITE(avg_lfk) AND FINITE(avg_hfk)))
ghigh_lm = WHERE(frest_lfkm GT wlh,ghlm)
ghigh_lp = WHERE(frest_lfkp GT wlh,ghlp)
ghigh_hm = WHERE(frest_hfkm GT wlh,ghhm)
ghigh_hp = WHERE(frest_hfkp GT wlh,ghhp)

glowf_lm = WHERE(frest_lfkm LE wlh,gllm)
glowf_lp = WHERE(frest_lfkp LE wlh,gllp)
glowf_hm = WHERE(frest_hfkm LE wlh,glhm)
glowf_hp = WHERE(frest_hfkp LE wlh,glhp)

PRINT,";", ghlm, ghlp, ghhm, ghhp, nvals
;         138         275         215         400         845
PRINT,";", gllm, gllp, glhm, glhp, nvals
;         293         139         216          14         845

PRINT, minmax(indexlm[glowf_lm]), minmax(indexlp[glowf_lp])
;       431000.44   2.9077398e+10
;       109843.03       2044587.9

PRINT, minmax(indexhm[glowf_hm]), minmax(indexhp[glowf_hp])
;       68233.225       11255488.
;       58536.467       82487.772


; => Plot data
wi,0
wi,1
wi,2

; => Cross-over frequency [pg. 105, Gurnett & Bhattacharjee, [2005]]
;wxf    = SQRT(2d0)*wcp/(wlh*SQRT(1d0 + (me/mp)^2))
;wcross = MEAN(wxf,/NAN,/DOUBLE)

; => Cross-over frequencies only apply when multiple ion species exist
;     => use wcp/wlh
wcross = SQRT(me/mp)

xran  = [0.01,4.00]
yran  = [1d4,1d10]
xttl  = 'k'+'!7q!3'+'!Dce!N (unitless)'
yttl  = 'n!U2!N (unitless)'
; => Minus Sign
xda0  = krhoelfm

yda2  = indexhm
; => Plus Sign
xda1  = krhoelfp
yda1  = indexlp

yda3  = indexhp

; => Minus Sign
xda0  = krhoelfm

xran  = [1e-4,15.0]

xttl  = '!7x!3'+'!Drest!N'+'/!7x!3'+'!Dlh!N (unitless)'

;-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
; => Look at envelope of data
;-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
xran  = [1e-4,15.0]
yran  = [1e-3,1d3]
xttl  = '!7x!3'+'!Drest!N'+'/!7x!3'+'!Dlh!N (unitless)'
yttl  = 'n!U2!N/n!DA!N'+'!U2!N (unitless)'
; => Minus Sign
xda0  = frest_lfkm/wlh
yda0  = indexlm/alfvinlm
xda2  = frest_hfkm/wlh
yda2  = indexhm/alfvinhm
; => Plus Sign
xda1  = frest_lfkp/wlh
yda1  = indexlp/alfvinlp
xda3  = frest_hfkp/wlh
yda3  = indexhp/alfvinhp
vertx = [1d0,1d0]*wcross[0]
;vertx = [1d0,1d0]*1d0/SQRT(mp/me)
verty = yran
vertl = '!7x!3'+'!Dx!N'+'/!7x!3'+'!Dlh!N'
horix = xran
horiy = [1d0,1d0]
horil = ''
xposi = 0.1
yposi = [5d2,1d2,5d1,1d1]
xx    = DINDGEN(500)*xran[1]/499L
yy    = -1d0*xx
fnam0 = 'whistler_dispersion_estimates_n2_nA2-vs-w_wlh_minus-sign'
fnam1 = 'whistler_dispersion_estimates_n2_nA2-vs-w_wlh_pluss-sign'
fnam2 = 'whistler_dispersion_estimates_n2_nA2-vs-w_wlh_both-signs'
;-------------------------------------------
pstr = {xrange:xran,yrange:yran,xtitle:xttl,ytitle:yttl,nodata:1,ylog:1,$
        xlog:1,ystyle:1,xstyle:1}

xo    = REFORM([xda0,xda2])
yo    = REFORM([yda0,yda2])
sp    = SORT(xo)
xo    = xo[sp]
yo    = yo[sp]
nn    = N_ELEMENTS(xo)
nchsz = 1.0
ochsz = !P.CHARSIZE
!P.CHARSIZE = nchsz
WSET,0
  PLOT,xda0,yda0,_EXTRA=pstr
    OPLOT,xda0,yda0,PSYM=3,SYMSIZE=10
; => Round the data points to fit to specific pixels
xydev = CONVERT_COORD(xo,yo,/DATA,/TO_DEVICE)
xdev  = REFORM(xydev[0,*])
ydev  = REFORM(xydev[1,*])
xdevl = ROUND(xdev)
ydevl = ROUND(ydev)
nwx   = !D.X_SIZE      ; => X-Axis size of Window (Device coordinates, e.g. pixels)
nwy   = !D.Y_SIZE      ; => Y-Axis size of Window (Device coordinates, e.g. pixels)
PRINT,';', nwx, nwy
;        1751        1069
xdev0 = [0L,nwx]
ydev0 = [0L,nwy]
xydat = CONVERT_COORD(xdev0,ydev0,/DEVICE,/TO_DATA)
; => Determine the data value per pixel in each direction as a scale
xdpx  = (xydat[0,1] - xydat[0,0])/(nwx - 1L)  ; => [X-Axis units]/[pixel]
ydpx  = (xydat[1,1] - xydat[1,0])/(nwy - 1L)  ; => [Y-Axis units]/[pixel]
PRINT,';', xdpx, ydpx, 1d0/xdpx, 1d0/ydpx
;   0.00974349      1.23119       102.63265      0.81222014

; => Determine the normal value per pixel in each direction as a scale
PRINT,';', 1d0/DOUBLE(nwx), 1d0/DOUBLE(nwy)
;   0.00057110223   0.00093545370

PRINT,';', !D.X_CH_SIZE, !D.Y_CH_SIZE
;           6          10
chsz  = str_size('.',1d0/DOUBLE(nwx))
PRINT,';', chsz, chsz*!D.X_CH_SIZE, chsz*!D.Y_CH_SIZE
;     0.250000      1.50000      2.50000
;xdevl = xdev - chsz*!D.X_CH_SIZE
;ydevl = ydev - chsz*!D.Y_CH_SIZE
;xdevu = xdev + chsz*!D.X_CH_SIZE
;ydevu = ydev + chsz*!D.Y_CH_SIZE


WSET,0
  PLOT,xda0,yda0,_EXTRA=pstr
    OPLOT,xda0,yda0,PSYM=3,SYMSIZE=10

aspect       = DOUBLE(nwx)/DOUBLE(nwy)
strTrialSize = 0.75
XYOUTS,0.5,0.5,/NORMAL,'.',WIDTH=twdthx,TEXT_AXES=0,CHARSIZE=-strTrialSize   ; => X = horizontal, Y = vertical
dotdev  = REFORM(CONVERT_COORD(twdthx[0],twdthx[0]*aspect[0],/NORMAL,/TO_DEVICE))
PRINT, ';',twdthx[0], dotdev[0], dotdev[1], dotdev[2]
;   0.00135261       2.3684210       2.3684210       0.0000000
chszx = dotdev[0]
chszy = dotdev[1]

;-------------------------------------------
;
; => Smear out data by the following method:
;
;   [(i-1),(j+1)]  [i,(j+1)]  [(i+1),(j+1)]
;
;     [(i-1),j]      [i,j]      [(i+1),j]
;
;   [(i-1),(j-1)]  [i,(j-1)]  [(i+1),(j-1)]
;
;-------------------------------------------
xdevl = xdev - chszx[0]
ydevl = ydev - chszy[0]
xdevu = xdev + chszx[0]
ydevu = ydev + chszy[0]

gel = 110
  ; => Top Row
  PLOTS,xdevl[gel[0]],ydevu[gel[0]],/DEVICE,PSYM=3,COLOR=250
  PLOTS, xdev[gel[0]],ydevu[gel[0]],/DEVICE,PSYM=3,COLOR=150
  PLOTS,xdevu[gel[0]],ydevu[gel[0]],/DEVICE,PSYM=3,COLOR= 50
  ; => Middle Row
  PLOTS,xdevl[gel[0]], ydev[gel[0]],/DEVICE,PSYM=3,COLOR=250
  PLOTS, xdev[gel[0]], ydev[gel[0]],/DEVICE,PSYM=3
  PLOTS,xdevu[gel[0]], ydev[gel[0]],/DEVICE,PSYM=3,COLOR= 50
  ; => Bottom Row
  PLOTS,xdevl[gel[0]],ydevl[gel[0]],/DEVICE,PSYM=3,COLOR=250
  PLOTS, xdev[gel[0]],ydevl[gel[0]],/DEVICE,PSYM=3,COLOR=150
  PLOTS,xdevu[gel[0]],ydevl[gel[0]],/DEVICE,PSYM=3,COLOR= 50


;-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
; => Plot ALL
;-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

WSET,0
  PLOT,xda0,yda0,_EXTRA=pstr
    OPLOT,xda0,yda0,PSYM=3,SYMSIZE=10

  ; => Top Row
  PLOTS,xdevl,ydevu,/DEVICE,PSYM=3,COLOR=250
  PLOTS, xdev,ydevu,/DEVICE,PSYM=3,COLOR=150
  PLOTS,xdevu,ydevu,/DEVICE,PSYM=3,COLOR= 50
  ; => Middle Row
  PLOTS,xdevl, ydev,/DEVICE,PSYM=3,COLOR=250
  PLOTS, xdev, ydev,/DEVICE,PSYM=3
  PLOTS,xdevu, ydev,/DEVICE,PSYM=3,COLOR= 50
  ; => Bottom Row
  PLOTS,xdevl,ydevl,/DEVICE,PSYM=3,COLOR=250
  PLOTS, xdev,ydevl,/DEVICE,PSYM=3,COLOR=150
  PLOTS,xdevu,ydevl,/DEVICE,PSYM=3,COLOR= 50

; => Smear out to 2 places
;
;   [(i-2),(j+2)]   [(i-1),(j+2)]  [i,(j+2)]  [(i+1),(j+2)]  [(i+2),(j+2)]
;
;   [(i-2),(j+1)]   [(i-1),(j+1)]  [i,(j+1)]  [(i+1),(j+1)]  [(i+2),(j+1)]
;
;     [(i-2),j]       [(i-1),j]      [i,j]      [(i+1),j]      [(i+2),j]
;
;   [(i-2),(j-1)]   [(i-1),(j-1)]  [i,(j-1)]  [(i+1),(j-1)]  [(i+2),(j-1)]
;
;   [(i-2),(j-2)]   [(i-1),(j-2)]  [i,(j-2)]  [(i+1),(j-2)]  [(i+2),(j-2)]
;


nsmear = 10L
delx   = chszx[0]
dely   = chszy[0]
dim2   = 2L*nsmear + 1L
xdeva  = DBLARR(nn,dim2)
ydeva  = DBLARR(nn,dim2)

FOR j=0L, dim2 - 1L DO BEGIN             $
  k          = j - nsmear              & $
  xdeva[*,j] = xdev[*] + k[0]*delx[0]  & $
  ydeva[*,j] = ydev[*] + k[0]*dely[0]

lcol = LINDGEN(dim2)*(250L - 30L)/(dim2 - 1L) + 30L
cols = lcol # REPLICATE(1L,dim2)
cols[dim2/2L,dim2/2L] = 255

WSET,0
  PLOT,xda0,yda0,_EXTRA=pstr
    OPLOT,xda0,yda0,PSYM=3,SYMSIZE=10

FOR j=0L, dim2 - 1L DO BEGIN                  $
  FOR k=0L, dim2 - 1L DO BEGIN                  $
  PLOTS,xdeva[*,j],ydeva[*,k],/DEVICE,PSYM=3,COLOR=cols[j,k]


;FOR j=0L, dim2 DO BEGIN
;  k          = j - nsmear
;  xdeva[*,j] = xdev[*] + k[0]*delx[0]
;  ydeva[*,j] = ydev[*] + k[0]*dely[0]
;ENDFOR

v1     = xda0
mn1    = 0.001d0
mx1    = 1d1
v2     = yda0
mn2    = 0.002d0
mx2    = 1d3
; => Want 200 bins in each direction
bin1   = (mx1[0] - mn1[0])/2d2
bin2   = (mx2[0] - mn2[0])/2d2
PRINT,';', bin1, bin2
;     0.049995000       4.9999900
result = HIST_2D(v1,v2,BIN1=bin1,BIN2=bin2,MIN1=mn1,MAX1=mx1,MIN2=mn2,MAX2=mx2)
PRINT,';', minmax(result[0,*])
;           0           9
PRINT,';', minmax(result[1,*])
;           0          55

;-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
; => Constants
;-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
f        = !VALUES.F_NAN
d        = !VALUES.D_NAN
c        = 2.99792458d8      ; -Speed of light in vacuum (m/s)
kB       = 1.380658d-23      ; -Boltzmann Constant (J/K)
epo      = 8.854187817d-12   ; -Permittivity of free space (F/m)
muo      = 4d0*!DPI*1d-7     ; -Permeability of free space (N/A^2 or H/m)
me       = 9.1093897d-31     ; -Electron mass (kg)
mp       = 1.6726231d-27     ; -Proton mass (kg)
qq       = 1.60217733d-19    ; => Fundamental charge (C)

date     = '121097'
test0    = tdss_lhw_stats_read(DATE=date)

date     = '082698'
test1    = tdss_lhw_stats_read(DATE=date)

date     = '092498'
test2    = tdss_lhw_stats_read(DATE=date)

date     = '021100'
test3    = tdss_lhw_stats_read(DATE=date)


; => Look at cold plasma theory
ndat     = 1000L
magf0    = (test0.MAGF_ST + test0.MAGF_EN)/2d0
dens0    = (test0.NE_SE[*,0] + test0.NE_SE[*,1])/2d0
bmag0    = SQRT(TOTAL(magf0^2,2L,/NAN))
freql    = test0.FREQ_LOW_HIGH[*,0]
freqh    = test0.FREQ_LOW_HIGH[*,1]
thkb0    = (test0.THETA_KB[*,0] + test0.THETA_KB[*,1])/2d0
freqf    = [freql[0],freqh[0]]
temp     = cold_plasma_params(bmag0[0],dens0[0],FREQF=freqf,NDAT=ndat)
; => minimize to determine relevant array element
diffa    = ABS(thkb0[0] - temp.ANGLES)
mnang    = MIN(diffa,/NAN,ln)
PRINT,";", ln, mnang, temp.ANGLES[ln], thkb0[0]
;         736    0.0053038039       66.306306       66.301003
PRINT,";", temp.CONE_ANG
;       89.631358       87.369416

sterms0  = temp.S_TERM
dterms0  = temp.D_TERM
pterms0  = temp.P_TERM
rterms0  = temp.R_TERM
lterms0  = temp.L_TERM
index00  = REFORM(temp.INDEX_REF_0[*,ln])
index10  = REFORM(temp.INDEX_REF_1[*,ln])

; => Calculate (|B|/E_{o})^2 and (|E|/E_{o})^2 from Mosier and Gurnett, [1971]
;      and Lengyel-Frey et al., [1994] {Eqs. 3 and 4}
theta    = thkb0[0]*!DPI/18d1
ctheta   = COS(theta)
stheta   = SIN(theta)
fac100   = (dterms0/(sterms0 - index00))
fac200   = (pterms0*ctheta)/(pterms0 - index00*stheta^2)
fac300   = (index00*ctheta*stheta)/(pterms0 - index00*stheta^2)

fac110   = (dterms0/(sterms0 - index10))
fac210   = (pterms0*ctheta)/(pterms0 - index10*stheta^2)
fac310   = (index10*ctheta*stheta)/(pterms0 - index10*stheta^2)
; => Squared values
BoverE00 = index00*(fac100^2 + fac200^2)
BoverE10 = index10*(fac110^2 + fac210^2)

PRINT,";", BoverE00
;(      0.00000,     -997166.)(      0.00000,     -128592.)
PRINT,";", BoverE10
;       910907.17       107089.75

EoverE00 = (1d0 + fac100^2 + fac300^2)
EoverE10 = (1d0 + fac110^2 + fac310^2)

PRINT,";", EoverE00
;       1.1395427       1.1957241
PRINT,";", EoverE10
;       1.1881006       1.1335895

IF (BoverE00[0] LT 0.) THEN BoverE00 = COMPLEX(0d0,BoverE00)


PRINT,";", SQRT(EoverE00)
;       1.0674937       1.0934917
PRINT,";", SQRT(EoverE10)
;       1.0900003       1.0647016

PRINT,";", SQRT(BoverE00)
;(      706.104,     -706.104)(      253.567,     -253.567)
PRINT,";", SQRT(BoverE10)
;       954.41457       327.24570



; => Try to convert observed B-fields to E-fields by inverting/substituting values
;      in equations
bo   = 19d-9  ; => (T)
fac0 = index10*(fac110^2 + fac210^2)
fac1 = (1d0 + fac110^2 + fac310^2)
eo2  = ((c*bo)^2)*fac1/fac0
PRINT,";", SQRT(eo2)*1d3
; => |E| (mV/m)
;       6.5052478       18.532255


; => Calculate the ratio of fluctuating E-field to B-field
fac0  = index10*(fac110^2 + fac210^2)
fac1  = (1d0 + fac110^2 + fac310^2)
rat10 = c^2*fac1/fac0

PRINT,";", SQRT(rat10)
;       342381.46       975381.82


; => Calculate the ratio of fluctuating E-field to B-field energy densities
fac0  = index10*(fac110^2 + fac210^2)
fac1  = (1d0 + fac110^2 + fac310^2)
rat10 = fac1/fac0
PRINT,";", SQRT(rat10)
;    0.0011420616    0.0032535236

;-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
; => Cold Plasma E-field Estimates
;-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
date     = '121097'
test0    = tdss_lhw_stats_read(DATE=date)

date     = '082698'
test1    = tdss_lhw_stats_read(DATE=date)

date     = '092498'
test2    = tdss_lhw_stats_read(DATE=date)

date     = '021100'

magf0    = (test0.MAGF_ST + test0.MAGF_EN)/2d0

freql    = test0.FREQ_LOW_HIGH[*,0]
freqh    = test0.FREQ_LOW_HIGH[*,1]
thkb0    = (test0.THETA_KB[*,0] + test0.THETA_KB[*,1])/2d0
amp0     = test0.PEAK_AMP[0]*1d0
temp000l =  cold_plasma_etob_ratio(bmag0[0],dens0[0],FREQF=freql[0],ANGLE=thkb0[0],MAGF=amp0)
PRINT,";", ABS(temp000l.(0)[0]), ABS(temp000l.(1)[0])
;       2.4331827       2.5994220


temp000h =  cold_plasma_etob_ratio(bmag0[0],dens0[0],FREQF=freqh[0],ANGLE=thkb0[0],MAGF=amp0)
PRINT,";", ABS(temp000h.(0)[0]), ABS(temp000h.(1)[0])
;       6.9407035       7.4051862



evn10    = test1.EVENT_N[0]
good     = WHERE(test1.EVENT_N EQ evn10[0],gd)
PRINT, ";", gd
;          36
magf1    = (test1.MAGF_ST + test1.MAGF_EN)/2d0
dens1    = (test1.NE_SE[*,0] + test1.NE_SE[*,1])/2d0
bmag1    = SQRT(TOTAL(magf1^2,2L,/NAN))
freql    = test1.FREQ_LOW_HIGH[*,0]
freqh    = test1.FREQ_LOW_HIGH[*,1]
thkb1    = (test1.THETA_KB[*,0] + test1.THETA_KB[*,1])/2d0
amp1     = test1.PEAK_AMP[0]*1d0
thkb190  = thkb1 < (18d1 - thkb1)
PRINT, ";", MEAN(thkb190[good],/NAN), STDDEV(thkb190[good],/NAN), $
            MIN(thkb190[good],/NAN), MAX(thkb190[good],/NAN)
;       53.133973       29.406249       11.214500       88.159500

good     = WHERE(freql EQ freql[1] AND freqh EQ freqh[1],gd)
PRINT, ";", gd
;           8


temp010l =  cold_plasma_etob_ratio(bmag1[1],dens1[1],FREQF=freql[1],ANGLE=thkb1[1],MAGF=amp1)
temp010h =  cold_plasma_etob_ratio(bmag1[1],dens1[1],FREQF=freqh[1],ANGLE=thkb1[1],MAGF=amp1)
PRINT,";", ABS(temp010l.(0)[0]), ABS(temp010l.(1)[0])
; => E-field (mV/m) estimate for 1998-08-26/06:40:26.120 UT, f =  7.0 Hz, theta_kB = 83.49 deg
;       18.307530       20.772607
PRINT,";", ABS(temp010h.(0)[0]), ABS(temp010h.(1)[0])
; => E-field (mV/m) estimate for 1998-08-26/06:40:26.120 UT, f = 30.0 Hz, theta_kB = 83.49 deg
;       33.349134       57.953084


; => From theory, we have the Poynting Flux, Sp = 1/2 Re[E x B*]
;      Sp = (c <|B|^2> Cos[theta])/(mu_o n)






pref    = ' => E-field (mV/m) estimate for '
mid0    = ' UT, f = '
mid1    = ' Hz, theta_kB = '
nn1     = N_ELEMENTS(test1.EVENT_N)
scet1   = test1.SCET_SE[*,0]
thkb190 = thkb1 < (18d1 - thkb1)
flows   = STRTRIM(STRING(FORMAT='(f10.1)',freql),2L)
fhighs  = STRTRIM(STRING(FORMAT='(f10.1)',freqh),2L)
thkbss  = STRTRIM(STRING(FORMAT='(f12.2)',thkb190),2L)
ampss   = STRTRIM(STRING(FORMAT='(f12.2)',test1.PEAK_AMP),2L)
short0  = WHERE(STRLEN(ampss) LT 5,sh0)
IF (sh0 GT 0) THEN ampss[short0] = ' '+ampss[short0]
suffx0  = ', Assuming |B| = '+ampss+' nT'
; => Add blank spaces to front of strings to keep the same columnated format
short0  = WHERE(STRLEN(flows) LE 3,sh0)
IF (sh0 GT 0) THEN flows[short0] = ' '+flows[short0]
short0  = WHERE(STRLEN(flows) LE 4,sh0)
IF (sh0 GT 0) THEN flows[short0] = ' '+flows[short0]
short0  = WHERE(STRLEN(fhighs) LE 3,sh0)
IF (sh0 GT 0) THEN fhighs[short0] = ' '+fhighs[short0]
short0  = WHERE(STRLEN(fhighs) LE 4,sh0)
IF (sh0 GT 0) THEN fhighs[short0] = ' '+fhighs[short0]
short0  = WHERE(STRLEN(thkbss) LT 5,sh0)
IF (sh0 GT 0) THEN thkbss[short0] = ' '+thkbss[short0]


FOR j=0L, nn1 - 1L DO BEGIN                                                                          $
  fl0s    = flows[j]                                                                               & $
  fh0s    = fhighs[j]                                                                              & $
  th0s    = thkbss[j]                                                                              & $
  stringl = pref[0]+scet1[j]+mid0[0]+fl0s[0]+mid1[0]+th0s[0]+' deg'+suffx0[j]                      & $
  stringh = pref[0]+scet1[j]+mid0[0]+fh0s[0]+mid1[0]+th0s[0]+' deg'+suffx0[j]                      & $
  amp00   = test1.PEAK_AMP[j]*1d0                                                                  & $
  templ   = cold_plasma_etob_ratio(bmag1[j],dens1[j],FREQF=freql[j],ANGLE=thkb190[j],MAGF=amp00)   & $
  temph   = cold_plasma_etob_ratio(bmag1[j],dens1[j],FREQF=freqh[j],ANGLE=thkb190[j],MAGF=amp00)   & $
  efssl   = ' '+STRTRIM(STRING(FORMAT='(f15.3)',ABS(templ.(1)[0])),2L)                             & $
  efssh   = ' '+STRTRIM(STRING(FORMAT='(f15.3)',ABS(temph.(1)[0])),2L)                             & $
  IF (STRLEN(efssl[0]) LE 7) THEN efssl[0] = ' '+efssl[0]                                          & $
  IF (STRLEN(efssl[0]) LT 8) THEN efssl[0] = ' '+efssl[0]                                          & $
  IF (STRLEN(efssh[0]) LE 7) THEN efssh[0] = ' '+efssh[0]                                          & $
  IF (STRLEN(efssh[0]) LT 8) THEN efssh[0] = ' '+efssh[0]                                          & $
  PRINT,";", efssl[0], stringl[0]                                                                  & $
  PRINT,";", efssh[0], stringh[0]

;   2.509 => E-field (mV/m) estimate for 1998-08-26/06:42:09.131 UT, f =  50.0 Hz, theta_kB =  7.82 deg, Assuming |B| =  1.96 nT
;   4.186 => E-field (mV/m) estimate for 1998-08-26/06:42:09.131 UT, f = 200.0 Hz, theta_kB =  7.82 deg, Assuming |B| =  1.96 nT
;   2.509 => E-field (mV/m) estimate for 1998-08-26/06:42:09.131 UT, f =  50.0 Hz, theta_kB =  7.65 deg, Assuming |B| =  1.96 nT
;   4.185 => E-field (mV/m) estimate for 1998-08-26/06:42:09.131 UT, f = 200.0 Hz, theta_kB =  7.65 deg, Assuming |B| =  1.96 nT
;   2.511 => E-field (mV/m) estimate for 1998-08-26/06:42:09.131 UT, f =  50.0 Hz, theta_kB = 12.30 deg, Assuming |B| =  1.96 nT
;   4.215 => E-field (mV/m) estimate for 1998-08-26/06:42:09.131 UT, f = 200.0 Hz, theta_kB = 12.30 deg, Assuming |B| =  1.96 nT
;   2.516 => E-field (mV/m) estimate for 1998-08-26/06:42:09.131 UT, f =  50.0 Hz, theta_kB = 16.92 deg, Assuming |B| =  1.96 nT
;   4.262 => E-field (mV/m) estimate for 1998-08-26/06:42:09.131 UT, f = 200.0 Hz, theta_kB = 16.92 deg, Assuming |B| =  1.96 nT
;   2.515 => E-field (mV/m) estimate for 1998-08-26/06:42:09.131 UT, f =  50.0 Hz, theta_kB = 16.35 deg, Assuming |B| =  1.96 nT
;   4.255 => E-field (mV/m) estimate for 1998-08-26/06:42:09.131 UT, f = 200.0 Hz, theta_kB = 16.35 deg, Assuming |B| =  1.96 nT




;-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
; => Estimate the E-field from rest frame frequencies and cold plasma disp.
;-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
f        = !VALUES.F_NAN
d        = !VALUES.D_NAN
c        = 2.99792458d8      ; -Speed of light in vacuum (m/s)
kB       = 1.380658d-23      ; -Boltzmann Constant (J/K)
epo      = 8.854187817d-12   ; -Permittivity of free space (F/m)
muo      = 4d0*!DPI*1d-7     ; -Permeability of free space (N/A^2 or H/m)
me       = 9.1093897d-31     ; -Electron mass (kg)
mp       = 1.6726231d-27     ; -Proton mass (kg)
qq       = 1.60217733d-19    ; => Fundamental charge (C)


date     = '121097'
test0    = tdss_lhw_stats_read(DATE=date)
scets0   = test0.SCET_SE[*,0]
avg_lfk0 = (test0.K_ST_LOWF_MP + test0.K_EN_LOWF_MP)/2d0
avg_hfk0 = (test0.K_ST_highF_MP + test0.K_EN_highF_MP)/2d0
freql0   = test0.FREQ_LOW_HIGH[*,0]
freqh0   = test0.FREQ_LOW_HIGH[*,1]
thkb0    = test0.THETA_KB
thkv0    = test0.THETA_KV
pkamp0   = test0.PEAK_AMP
wce0     = (test0.WCE_SE[*,0] + test0.WCE_SE[*,1])/2d0
wpe0     = (test0.WPE_SE[*,0] + test0.WPE_SE[*,1])/2d0
thkb0    = (thkb0) < (18d1 - thkb0)
thkv0    = (thkv0) < (18d1 - thkv0)
thkb0    = (thkb0[*,0] + thkb0[*,1])/2d0
thkv0    = (thkv0[*,0] + thkv0[*,1])/2d0
magf0    = (test0.MAGF_ST + test0.MAGF_EN)/2d0
dens0    = (test0.NE_SE[*,0] + test0.NE_SE[*,1])/2d0
bmag0    = SQRT(TOTAL(magf0^2,2L,/NAN))

date     = '082698'
test1    = tdss_lhw_stats_read(DATE=date)
scets1   = test1.SCET_SE[*,0]
avg_lfk1 = (test1.K_ST_LOWF_MP + test1.K_EN_LOWF_MP)/2d0
avg_hfk1 = (test1.K_ST_highF_MP + test1.K_EN_highF_MP)/2d0
freql1   = test1.FREQ_LOW_HIGH[*,0]
freqh1   = test1.FREQ_LOW_HIGH[*,1]
thkb1    = test1.THETA_KB
thkv1    = test1.THETA_KV
pkamp1   = test1.PEAK_AMP
wce1     = (test1.WCE_SE[*,0] + test1.WCE_SE[*,1])/2d0
wpe1     = (test1.WPE_SE[*,0] + test1.WPE_SE[*,1])/2d0
thkb1    = (thkb1) < (18d1 - thkb1)
thkv1    = (thkv1) < (18d1 - thkv1)
thkb1    = (thkb1[*,0] + thkb1[*,1])/2d0
thkv1    = (thkv1[*,0] + thkv1[*,1])/2d0
magf1    = (test1.MAGF_ST + test1.MAGF_EN)/2d0
dens1    = (test1.NE_SE[*,0] + test1.NE_SE[*,1])/2d0
bmag1    = SQRT(TOTAL(magf1^2,2L,/NAN))

date     = '092498'
test2    = tdss_lhw_stats_read(DATE=date)
scets2   = test2.SCET_SE[*,0]
avg_lfk2 = (test2.K_ST_LOWF_MP + test2.K_EN_LOWF_MP)/2d0
avg_hfk2 = (test2.K_ST_highF_MP + test2.K_EN_highF_MP)/2d0
freql2   = test2.FREQ_LOW_HIGH[*,0]
freqh2   = test2.FREQ_LOW_HIGH[*,1]
thkb2    = test2.THETA_KB
thkv2    = test2.THETA_KV
pkamp2   = test2.PEAK_AMP
wce2     = (test2.WCE_SE[*,0] + test2.WCE_SE[*,1])/2d0
wpe2     = (test2.WPE_SE[*,0] + test2.WPE_SE[*,1])/2d0
thkb2    = (thkb2) < (18d1 - thkb2)
thkv2    = (thkv2) < (18d1 - thkv2)
thkb2    = (thkb2[*,0] + thkb2[*,1])/2d0
thkv2    = (thkv2[*,0] + thkv2[*,1])/2d0
magf2    = (test2.MAGF_ST + test2.MAGF_EN)/2d0
dens2    = (test2.NE_SE[*,0] + test2.NE_SE[*,1])/2d0
bmag2    = SQRT(TOTAL(magf2^2,2L,/NAN))

date     = '021100'
test3    = tdss_lhw_stats_read(DATE=date)
scets3   = test3.SCET_SE[*,0]
avg_lfk3 = (test3.K_ST_LOWF_MP + test3.K_EN_LOWF_MP)/2d0
avg_hfk3 = (test3.K_ST_highF_MP + test3.K_EN_highF_MP)/2d0
freql3   = test3.FREQ_LOW_HIGH[*,0]
freqh3   = test3.FREQ_LOW_HIGH[*,1]
thkb3    = test3.THETA_KB
thkv3    = test3.THETA_KV
pkamp3   = test3.PEAK_AMP
wce3     = (test3.WCE_SE[*,0] + test3.WCE_SE[*,1])/2d0
wpe3     = (test3.WPE_SE[*,0] + test3.WPE_SE[*,1])/2d0
thkb3    = (thkb3) < (18d1 - thkb3)
thkv3    = (thkv3) < (18d1 - thkv3)
thkb3    = (thkb3[*,0] + thkb3[*,1])/2d0
thkv3    = (thkv3[*,0] + thkv3[*,1])/2d0
magf3    = (test3.MAGF_ST + test3.MAGF_EN)/2d0
dens3    = (test3.NE_SE[*,0] + test3.NE_SE[*,1])/2d0
bmag3    = SQRT(TOTAL(magf3^2,2L,/NAN))
;-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
; => Combine terms
;-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
thkb     = [thkb0,thkb1,thkb2,thkb3]
thkv     = [thkv0,thkv1,thkv2,thkv3]
wce      = [wce0,wce1,wce2,wce3]
wpe      = [wpe0,wpe1,wpe2,wpe3]
avg_lfk  = [avg_lfk0,avg_lfk1,avg_lfk2,avg_lfk3]
avg_hfk  = [avg_hfk0,avg_hfk1,avg_hfk2,avg_hfk3]
scets    = [scets0,scets1,scets2,scets3]
pkamp    = [pkamp0,pkamp1,pkamp2,pkamp3]
dens     = [dens0,dens1,dens2,dens3]
bmag     = [bmag0,bmag1,bmag2,bmag3]

; => Separate by plus and minus sign
avg_lfkm = avg_lfk[*,0]
avg_lfkp = avg_lfk[*,1]
avg_hfkm = avg_hfk[*,0]
avg_hfkp = avg_hfk[*,1]
; => Calculate rest frame frequencies
ckm        = (c*1d-3)
fac0       = ckm^2*wce*COS(thkb*!DPI/18d1)
frest_lfkm = avg_lfkm^2*fac0/(wpe^2 + (avg_lfkm*ckm)^2)
frest_lfkp = avg_lfkp^2*fac0/(wpe^2 + (avg_lfkp*ckm)^2)
frest_hfkm = avg_hfkm^2*fac0/(wpe^2 + (avg_hfkm*ckm)^2)
frest_hfkp = avg_hfkp^2*fac0/(wpe^2 + (avg_hfkp*ckm)^2)
; => Calculate index of refraction
indexlm  = (avg_lfkm*ckm)^2/(frest_lfkm)^2
indexlp  = (avg_lfkp*ckm)^2/(frest_lfkp)^2
indexhm  = (avg_hfkm*ckm)^2/(frest_hfkm)^2
indexhp  = (avg_hfkp*ckm)^2/(frest_hfkp)^2

bad      = WHERE(FINITE(frest_lfkm) EQ 0,bd)
IF (bd GT 0) THEN frest_lfkm[bad] = 0d0
bad      = WHERE(FINITE(frest_lfkp) EQ 0,bd)
IF (bd GT 0) THEN frest_lfkp[bad] = 0d0
bad      = WHERE(FINITE(frest_hfkm) EQ 0,bd)
IF (bd GT 0) THEN frest_hfkm[bad] = 0d0
bad      = WHERE(FINITE(frest_hfkp) EQ 0,bd)
IF (bd GT 0) THEN frest_hfkp[bad] = 0d0




nn1     = N_ELEMENTS(thkb)
thkb190 = thkb
flowm   = STRTRIM(STRING(FORMAT='(f10.1)',frest_lfkm/(2d0*!DPI)),2L)
flowp   = STRTRIM(STRING(FORMAT='(f10.1)',frest_lfkp/(2d0*!DPI)),2L)
fhighm  = STRTRIM(STRING(FORMAT='(f10.1)',frest_hfkm/(2d0*!DPI)),2L)
fhighp  = STRTRIM(STRING(FORMAT='(f10.1)',frest_hfkp/(2d0*!DPI)),2L)
; => Add blank spaces to front of strings to keep the same columnated format
short0  = WHERE(STRLEN(flowm) LE 3,sh0)
IF (sh0 GT 0) THEN flowm[short0] = ' '+flowm[short0]
short0  = WHERE(STRLEN(flowm) LE 4,sh0)
IF (sh0 GT 0) THEN flowm[short0] = ' '+flowm[short0]
short0  = WHERE(STRLEN(flowp) LE 3,sh0)
IF (sh0 GT 0) THEN flowp[short0] = ' '+flowp[short0]
short0  = WHERE(STRLEN(flowp) LE 4,sh0)
IF (sh0 GT 0) THEN flowp[short0] = ' '+flowp[short0]
short0  = WHERE(STRLEN(fhighm) LE 3,sh0)
IF (sh0 GT 0) THEN fhighm[short0] = ' '+fhighm[short0]
short0  = WHERE(STRLEN(fhighm) LE 4,sh0)
IF (sh0 GT 0) THEN fhighm[short0] = ' '+fhighm[short0]
short0  = WHERE(STRLEN(fhighp) LE 3,sh0)
IF (sh0 GT 0) THEN fhighp[short0] = ' '+fhighp[short0]
short0  = WHERE(STRLEN(fhighp) LE 4,sh0)
IF (sh0 GT 0) THEN fhighp[short0] = ' '+fhighp[short0]

thkbss  = STRTRIM(STRING(FORMAT='(f12.2)',thkb190),2L)
short0  = WHERE(STRLEN(thkbss) LT 5,sh0)
IF (sh0 GT 0) THEN thkbss[short0] = ' '+thkbss[short0]
ampss   = STRTRIM(STRING(FORMAT='(f12.2)',pkamp),2L)
short0  = WHERE(STRLEN(ampss) LT 5,sh0)
IF (sh0 GT 0) THEN ampss[short0] = ' '+ampss[short0]
suffx0  = ', Assuming |B| = '+ampss+' nT'



pref    = ' => E-field (mV/m) estimate for '
mid0m   = ' UT, f_rest(-) = '
mid0p   = ' UT, f_rest(+) = '
mid1    = ' Hz, theta_kB = '
FOR j=0L, nn1 - 1L DO BEGIN                                                                           $
  fl0m     = flowm[j]                                                                               & $
  fl0p     = flowp[j]                                                                               & $
  fh0m     = fhighm[j]                                                                              & $
  fh0p     = fhighp[j]                                                                              & $
  th0s     = thkbss[j]                                                                              & $
  freqlm   = frest_lfkm[j]/(2d0*!DPI)                                                               & $
  freqlp   = frest_lfkp[j]/(2d0*!DPI)                                                               & $
  freqhm   = frest_hfkm[j]/(2d0*!DPI)                                                               & $
  freqhp   = frest_hfkp[j]/(2d0*!DPI)                                                               & $
  stringlm = pref[0]+scets[j]+mid0m[0]+fl0m[0]+mid1[0]+th0s[0]+' deg'+suffx0[j]                     & $
  stringlp = pref[0]+scets[j]+mid0p[0]+fl0p[0]+mid1[0]+th0s[0]+' deg'+suffx0[j]                     & $
  stringhm = pref[0]+scets[j]+mid0m[0]+fh0m[0]+mid1[0]+th0s[0]+' deg'+suffx0[j]                     & $
  stringhp = pref[0]+scets[j]+mid0p[0]+fh0p[0]+mid1[0]+th0s[0]+' deg'+suffx0[j]                     & $
  amp00    = pkamp[j]*1d0                                                                           & $
  templm   = cold_plasma_etob_ratio(bmag[j],dens[j],FREQF=freqlm[0],ANGLE=thkb190[j],MAGF=amp00)    & $
  templp   = cold_plasma_etob_ratio(bmag[j],dens[j],FREQF=freqlp[0],ANGLE=thkb190[j],MAGF=amp00)    & $
  temphm   = cold_plasma_etob_ratio(bmag[j],dens[j],FREQF=freqhm[0],ANGLE=thkb190[j],MAGF=amp00)    & $
  temphp   = cold_plasma_etob_ratio(bmag[j],dens[j],FREQF=freqhp[0],ANGLE=thkb190[j],MAGF=amp00)    & $
  IF (FINITE(ABS(templm.(1)[0])) EQ 0) THEN eamplm = 0d0 ELSE eamplm = ABS(templm.(1)[0])           & $
  IF (FINITE(ABS(templp.(1)[0])) EQ 0) THEN eamplp = 0d0 ELSE eamplp = ABS(templp.(1)[0])           & $
  IF (FINITE(ABS(temphm.(1)[0])) EQ 0) THEN eamphm = 0d0 ELSE eamphm = ABS(temphm.(1)[0])           & $
  IF (FINITE(ABS(temphp.(1)[0])) EQ 0) THEN eamphp = 0d0 ELSE eamphp = ABS(temphp.(1)[0])           & $
  efsslm   = ' '+STRTRIM(STRING(FORMAT='(f15.3)',eamplm),2L)                                        & $
  efsslp   = ' '+STRTRIM(STRING(FORMAT='(f15.3)',eamplp),2L)                                        & $
  efsshm   = ' '+STRTRIM(STRING(FORMAT='(f15.3)',eamphm),2L)                                        & $
  efsshp   = ' '+STRTRIM(STRING(FORMAT='(f15.3)',eamphp),2L)                                        & $
  IF (STRLEN(efsslm[0]) LE 7) THEN efsslm[0] = ' '+efsslm[0]                                        & $
  IF (STRLEN(efsslm[0]) LT 8) THEN efsslm[0] = ' '+efsslm[0]                                        & $
  IF (STRLEN(efsslp[0]) LE 7) THEN efsslp[0] = ' '+efsslp[0]                                        & $
  IF (STRLEN(efsslp[0]) LT 8) THEN efsslp[0] = ' '+efsslp[0]                                        & $
  IF (STRLEN(efsshm[0]) LE 7) THEN efsshm[0] = ' '+efsshm[0]                                        & $
  IF (STRLEN(efsshm[0]) LT 8) THEN efsshm[0] = ' '+efsshm[0]                                        & $
  IF (STRLEN(efsshp[0]) LE 7) THEN efsshp[0] = ' '+efsshp[0]                                        & $
  IF (STRLEN(efsshp[0]) LT 8) THEN efsshp[0] = ' '+efsshp[0]                                        & $
  PRINT,";", efsslm[0], stringlm[0]                                                                 & $
  PRINT,";", efsslp[0], stringlp[0]                                                                 & $
  PRINT,";", efsshm[0], stringhm[0]                                                                 & $
  PRINT,";", efsshp[0], stringhp[0]
